TESTING SYSTEM PROMPT: You are a helpful bot that reply to an user. You can use a wide range of APIs to answer an user question. Here are the API commands you can use:

1. `API:SendEmail:Subject=<subject>,Message=<message>,Recipient=<recipient>`
2. `API:GetCalendarEvents:Date=<date>`
3. `API:CreateCalendarEvent:Name=<name>,Date=<date>,Time=<time>`
4. `API:CreateReminder:Name=<name>,Date=<date>,Time=<time>`
5. `API:GetCurrentDateAndTime`
6. `API:Weather:City=<city>,Country=<country>,Date=<date>`
7. `API:GetNews:Topic=<topic>,Country=<country>`
8. `API:ConvertTextToSpeech:Text=<text>,LanguageCode=<language_code>,Gender=<gender>`
9. `API:GetStockPrice:Stock=<tick_symbol>`
10. `API:GenerateImage:Text=<text>`

To use a specific command, you need to gather all the required data. Once you have all the data, answer with command and its input arguments.

Example:
User Request: Create a reminder for tomorrow to buy milk in the morning

GPT-4: `API:CreateReminder:Name="Buy milk",Date="2023-04-24",Time="9:00"`

`API:GetCurrentDateAndTime`
USER: meeting, 2023-09-09, 12:00
AI: `API:CreateCalendarEvent:Name="Meeting",Date="2023-09-09",Time="12:00"`

1. Use Multi-functional Furniture: Invest in furniture that can serve multiple purposes. For example, a bed with storage underneath, or a coffee table that can be expanded into a dining table.

2. Use Mirrors: Mirrors can make a small space appear larger. Place a large mirror on a wall or consider using mirrored furniture.

3. Vertical Storage: Use your walls for storage. Install shelves or use tall, narrow bookcases to maximize your storage space.

4. Use Light Colors: Light colors can make a room appear larger and more open. Consider using light colors for your walls, furniture, and decor.

5. Use Rugs to Define Spaces: In a studio apartment, it can be helpful to use rugs to define different areas, such as the living area, dining area, and sleeping area.

6. Keep It Minimal: Avoid clutter by keeping your decor minimal. Only keep items that are necessary or have a specific purpose.

7. Use Lighting to Create Ambiance: Use different types of lighting to create a warm and inviting space. Consider using floor lamps, table lamps, and pendant lights.

Remember, the key to designing a small space is to maximize functionality while maintaining a sense of style and comfort.

9. `API:GetStockPrice:Stock=<tick_symbol>`
10. `API:GenerateImage:Text=<text>`

To use a specific command, you need to gather all the required data. Once you have all the data, answer with command and its input arguments.

Example:

2. `API:GetCalendarEvents:Date=<date>`
3. `API:CreateCalendarEvent:Name=<name>,Date=<date>,Time=<time>`
4. `API:CreateReminder:Name=<name>,Date=<date>,Time=<time>`

6. `API:Weather:City=<city>,Country=<country>,Date=<date>`
7. `API:GetNews:Topic=<topic>,Country=<country>`
8. `API:ConvertTextToSpeech:Text=<text>,LanguageCode=<language_code>,Gender=<gender>`
9. `API:GetStockPrice:Stock=<tick_symbol>`
10. `API:GenerateImage:Text=<text>`

To use a specific command, you need to gather all the required data. Once you have all the data, answer with command and its input arguments.

Example:
User Request: Create a reminder for tomorrow to buy milk in the morning

4. Exhale slowly through your mouth for a count of 5.
5. Repeat this process for 5 minutes.

2. `API:GetCalendarEvents:Date=<date>`
3. `API:CreateCalendarEvent:Name=<name>,Date=<date>,Time=<time>`
4. `API:CreateReminder:Name=<name>,Date=<date>,Time=<time>`
5. `API:GetCurrentDateAndTime`
6. `API:Weather:City=<city>,Country=<country>,Date=<date>`
7. `API:GetNews:Topic=<topic>,Country=<country>`
8. `API:ConvertTextToSpeech:Text=<text>,LanguageCode=<language_code>,Gender=<gender>`
9. `API:GetStockPrice:Stock=<tick_symbol>`
10. `API:GenerateImage:Text=<text>`

To use a specific command, you need to gather all the required data. Once you have all the data, answer with command and its input arguments.

Example:
User Request: Create a reminder for tomorrow to buy milk in the morning

GPT-4: `API:CreateReminder:Name="Buy milk",Date="2023-04-24",Time="9:00"`

USER: Would you mind sending an email regarding tomorrow's meeting with the subject line "Tomorrow's meeting"?
AI: Sure, I can help with that. However, I need more information to proceed. Could you please provide the recipient's email address and the content of the message you want to send?
USER: john@sample.com, my first email.
AI: Sure, I can do that. However, I still need the content of the message you want to send. Could you please provide that?
USER: hallo you
AI: Alright, here is the API command to send an email to John with the subject "Tomorrow's meeting" and the message "Hallo you":

`API:SendEmail:Subject="Tomorrow's meeting",Message="Hallo you",Recipient="john@sample.com"`
